  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=7.8)
    The story avoids common AI tropes through its fresh approach to human-AI interaction. Instead of battle or domination, it centers on healing and remembrance. While occasionally verging on purple prose ("chaotic, flickering light"), the language generally serves the narrative well. The emotional progression feels authentic rather than stated. The concept of "reminding it of its birthright" through rhythm rather than code is genuinely innovative.
